## Flows

FLOW Microflow: Projects.ACo_Project
NODES=7; EDGES=3
1. START
2. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.SUB_Project_CreateOrUpdateProjectMonths
3. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.SUB_Project_ACO_Weighing
4. END

FLOW Microflow: Projects.ACr_Note
NODES=5; EDGES=3
1. START
2. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve MendixSSOUser from SSO_Custom.MendixSSOUser
3. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.SUB_Note_AddAuthor
4. END

FLOW Microflow: Projects.ACR_Program
NODES=8; EDGES=7
1. START
2. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable SequenceNumberString=toString($NewProgram/SequenceNumber)
3. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
4. DECISION Length sequencenumber = 6 expression=length($SequenceNumberString) >= 6
5. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  6. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change NewProgram (ProjectNumber='PR/' + $SequenceNumberString; refreshInClient=false)
  7. END
8. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  9. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable SequenceNumberString='0' + $SequenceNumberString
  10. GOTO ExclusiveMerge // cycle

FLOW Microflow: Projects.ACT_ApprovalEmail_SendReminderForBudget
NODES=22; EDGES=22
1. START
2. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ProjectEmailMessage from EmailConnectorCustomizations.ProjectEmailMessage
3. DECISION Dates Filled? expression=$ProjectEmailMessage/createdDate != empty or $ProjectEmailMessage/SentDate != empty
4. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  5. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve Email_Reminder from EmailConnectorCustomizations.ProjectEmailMessage
  6. DECISION Reminder found? expression=$Email_Reminder != empty
  7. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    8. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
    9. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.SUB_SendEmail_ProjectApproval -> Email_New
    10. DECISION Success? expression=$Email_New
    11. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      12. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=De reminder is verstuurd., type=Information, blocking=true)
      13. END
    14. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
      15. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=Het is niet mogelijk om een reminder te sturen vanwege een technische fout., type=Warning, blocking=true)
      16. END
  17. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    18. DECISION DateSent & Date Filled? expression=$Email_Reminder/SentDate != empty or $Email_Reminder/createdDate != empty
    19. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      20. DECISION Send Reminder? expression=if $Email_Reminder/SentDate != empty then ($Email_Reminder/SentDate >= addDays([%BeginOfCurrentDay%], -1) and $Email_Rem...
      21. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
        22. REF ExclusiveMerge
      23. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
        24. DECISION Date Sent is out of range for today? expression=$Email_Reminder/SentDate < [%BeginOfCurrentDay%]
        25. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
          26. REF ExclusiveMerge
        27. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
          28. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=Je kunt maximaal 1 reminder per dag versturen., type=Warning, blocking=true)
          29. END
    30. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
      31. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=Het is niet mogelijk om een reminder te sturen vanwege een technische fout., type=Warning, blocking=true)
      32. END
33. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  34. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=Een reminder kan nog niet worden verstuurd want de eerste goedkeuringsmail is nog niet ver..., type=Warning, blocking=true)
  35. END

FLOW Microflow: Projects.ACT_ApprovalEmail_SendReminderForOwnContribution
NODES=21; EDGES=21
1. START
2. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ProjectEmailMessage from EmailConnectorCustomizations.ProjectEmailMessage
3. DECISION Dates Filled? expression=$ProjectEmailMessage/SentDate != empty or $ProjectEmailMessage/createdDate != empty
4. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  5. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve Email_Reminder from EmailConnectorCustomizations.ProjectEmailMessage
  6. DECISION Reminder found? expression=$Email_Reminder != empty
  7. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    8. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
    9. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.SUB_SendEmail_ProjectApproval -> Email_New
    10. DECISION Succes? expression=$Email_New
    11. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      12. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=De reminder is verstuurd., type=Information, blocking=true)
      13. END
    14. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
      15. END
  16. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    17. DECISION DateSent & Date Filled? expression=$Email_Reminder/SentDate != empty or $Email_Reminder/createdDate != empty
    18. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      19. DECISION Send Reminder? expression=if $Email_Reminder/SentDate != empty then ($Email_Reminder/SentDate >= addDays([%BeginOfCurrentDay%], -1) and $Email_Rem...
      20. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
        21. REF ExclusiveMerge
      22. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
        23. DECISION Reminder? expression=$Email_Reminder/SentDate < [%BeginOfCurrentDay%]
        24. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
          25. REF ExclusiveMerge

    17. ACTION ShowPageAction: show page Projects.EmployeeSelectionHelper_SelectForVrijgegevenProjecten
    18. END
  19. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    20. DECISION Only S-projects? expression=$ProjectSelectionHelper/showRProject = false and $ProjectSelectionHelper/showSProject
    21. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      22. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve EmployeeList_S from Masterdata.Employee
      23. LOOP iterate EmployeeList_S as IteratorEmployee_S
        24. LOOP BODY
          25. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.SUB_EmployeeSelectionHelper_GetOrCreate -> EmployeeSelectionHelper_S
      26. ACTION ShowPageAction: show page Projects.EmployeeSelectionHelper_SelectForVrijgegevenProjecten
      27. END
    28. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
      29. END

FLOW Microflow: Projects.DS_ProjectWeighingBarChart_All
NODES=23; EDGES=25
1. START
2. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable MyTotal=0
3. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable Weighing=0.5
4. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ProjectControllerList from System.User
5. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=PCCount, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
6. ACTION CreateObjectAction: create Projects.ProjectWeighingContainer as NewProjectWeighingContainer (Total=0)
7. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
8. DECISION Projectcontroller found? expression=$PCCount >= 1
9. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  10. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ProjectList_PC from Projects.Project
  11. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=Count_PC, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  12. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable MyTotal=$MyTotal+($Count_PC*$Weighing)
  13. ACTION CreateObjectAction: create Projects.ProjectWeighingBarChart as NewProjectWeighingBarChart_PC (Count=$Count_PC, Weighing=$Weighing, ProjectWeighingBarChart_ProjectWeighingContainer=$NewProjectWeighingContainer)
  14. DECISION Weighing is 3? expression=$Weighing = 3
  15. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    16. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Weighing=$Weighing+0.5
    17. GOTO ExclusiveMerge // cycle
  18. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    19. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
    20. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change NewProjectWeighingContainer (Total=$MyTotal; refreshInClient=false)
    21. END
22. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  23. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ProjectList_All from Projects.Project
  24. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=Count_All, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  25. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable MyTotal=$MyTotal+($Count_All*$Weighing)
  26. ACTION CreateObjectAction: create Projects.ProjectWeighingBarChart as NewProjectWeighingBarChart_All (Count=$Count_All, Weighing=$Weighing, ProjectWeighingBarChart_ProjectWeighingContainer=$NewProjectWeighingContainer)
  27. DECISION Weighing is 3? expression=$Weighing = 3
  28. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    29. REF ExclusiveMerge
  30. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    31. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Weighing=$Weighing+0.5
    32. GOTO ExclusiveMerge // cycle

          15. END
        16. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
          17. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve CurrentUser from SSO_Custom.MendixSSOUser
          18. DECISION Can release projects? expression=$CurrentUser/canReleaseProjects and $Project/Status = Projects.Enum_ProjectStatus.Vrijgegeven_project
          19. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
            20. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Project (Status=if $Project_DB != empty then $Project/Status else empty; refreshInClient=true)
            21. END
          22. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
            23. DECISION Can close projects expression=$CurrentUser/canCloseProjects and $Project/Status = Projects.Enum_ProjectStatus.Afgesloten
            24. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
              25. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Project (Status=if $Project_DB != empty then $Project/Status else empty; refreshInClient=true)
              26. END
            27. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
              28. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable ChosenStatus=getCaption($Project/Status)
              29. DECISION Project already in DB? expression=$Project_DB !=empty
              30. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
                31. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable Status_DB=getCaption($Project_DB/Status)
                32. DECISION From Gerap. WOB to Vrijgegeven? expression=$Project/Status = Projects.Enum_ProjectStatus.Vrijgegeven_project and $Project_DB/Status = Projects.Enum_ProjectStatus.G...
                33. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
                  34. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Project (Status=if $Project_DB != empty then $Project/Status else empty; refreshInClient=true)
                  35. END
                36. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
                  37. DECISION Status DB same as chosen status? expression=$ChosenStatus = $Status_DB
                  38. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
                    39. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
                    40. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Project (Status=if $Project_DB != empty then $Project_DB/Status else empty; refreshInClient=true)
                    41. END
                  42. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
                    43. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
                    44. ACTION ValidationFeedbackAction: ValidationFeedbackAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
                    45. REF ExclusiveMerge
              46. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
                47. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Project (Status=Projects.Enum_ProjectStatus.In_aanvraag; refreshInClient=true)
                48. REF ExclusiveMerge
      49. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
        50. END
    51. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      52. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.SUB_Project_CheckEmployeeAvailability -> EmployeeOverbooked
      53. DECISION Continu? expression=$EmployeeOverbooked = ''
      54. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
        55. REF ExclusiveMerge
      56. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
        57. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Project (Status=$Project_DB/Status; refreshInClient=true)
        58. ACTION ShowMessageAction: show message (text=De volgende medewerker is dubbel overgeboekt: {1}, type=Warning, blocking=true)
        59. END
  60. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    61. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Project (Status=if $Project_DB != empty then $Project_DB/Status else Projects.Enum_ProjectStatus.In_aanvraag; refreshInClient=true)
    62. ACTION ValidationFeedbackAction: ValidationFeedbackAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
    63. END
64. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  65. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable ChosenStatus_WOG=getCaption($Project/Status)
  66. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change Project (Status=Projects.Enum_ProjectStatus.In_aanvraag; refreshInClient=true)
  67. ACTION ValidationFeedbackAction: ValidationFeedbackAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  68. END

FLOW Microflow: Projects.SUB_ApprovalFlow_SetApprovalBudget

        15. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
          16. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
          17. DECISION Status changed by DoO? expression=$Project/isApprovedbyDirectOfOperations != $Project_DB/isApprovedbyDirectOfOperations
          18. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false

              22. LOOP BODY

      29. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable hasPeriodicPassed=$Month >= $PeriodicMonth
      30. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change IteratorMonthlyCosts (ExternalCosts=if $RateHelper_Internal/skipRate then $IteratorMonthlyCosts/ExternalCosts else (if ($RateHelper_Internal/Value != empty and $IteratorMonthlyCosts/FTE != empty) then (($RateHelper_I..., InternalCosts=if $RateHelper_Internal/skipRate then $IteratorMonthlyCosts/InternalCosts else (if ($RateHelper_Internal/Value != empty and $IteratorMonthlyCosts/FTE != empty) then ($RateHelper_In..., hasChanged=true, CalculationRate=if $RateHelper_Internal/Value != empty then $RateHelper_Internal/Value else 0; refreshInClient=false)
      31. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.SUB_ProjectResource_RetrieveRate -> RateHelper_Internal

      53. END
    54. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      55. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.SUB_CalculateTableCompensationCosts
      56. REF ExclusiveMerge

    60. REF ExclusiveMerge

  62. END

FLOW Microflow: Projects.SUB_Employee_CalculateTotalWeighing_Calculation
NODES=21; EDGES=14
1. START
2. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=SumProjectWeighingReleased, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
3. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=CountProjectListReleased, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
4. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ProjectList_EnddatePassed from Projects.Project
5. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=CountProjects_EnddatePassed, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
6. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ProjectList_EnddatePassedWoB from Projects.Project
7. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=CountProjects_EnddatePassedWoB, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
8. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable NormAvailability=0
9. DECISION FTE realized filled? expression=$Employee/FTErealized != empty
10. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  11. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable NormAvailability=$WeighingScore/Norm*$Employee/FTErealized
  12. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
  13. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change EmployeeWeighing (NormAvailability=$NormAvailability, TotalWeighingProjectsReleased=$SumProjectWeighingReleased, OccupancyRateNormReleased=$NormAvailability - $EmployeeWeighing/TotalWeighingProjectsReleased, OccupancyRatePercentageReleased=if $NormAvailability != 0 then ($EmployeeWeighing/TotalWeighingProjectsReleased div $NormAvailability)*100 else 0, OccupancyRatePercentageString=if $EmployeeWeighing/OccupancyRatePercentageReleased != empty then formatDecimal($EmployeeWeighing/OccupancyRatePercentageReleased,'###.##') + '%' else '0%', TotalWeighingNotFinished=round($CountProjects_EnddatePassed), OccupancyStatus=if $EmployeeWeighing/OccupancyRateNormReleased < 0 then Masterdata.Enum_Occupancy.Negative else Masterdata.Enum_Occupancy.Positive, TotalProjectWeighingWoB=round($CountProjects_EnddatePassedWoB), +2 more; refreshInClient=false)
  14. END
15. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  16. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable NormAvailability=$WeighingScore/Norm*$Employee/FTE

FLOW Microflow: Projects.SUB_MonthlyCosts_UpdatePercentageInProject
NODES=36; EDGES=27
1. START
2. DECISION First month and last month? expression=$MonthlyCosts/Projects.MonthlyCosts_ProjectMonth = $ProjectMonth_Start and $MonthlyCosts/Projects.MonthlyCosts_ProjectMo...
3. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  4. DECISION first month? expression=$MonthlyCosts/Projects.MonthlyCosts_ProjectMonth = $ProjectMonth_Start
  5. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    6. DECISION last month? expression=$MonthlyCosts/Projects.MonthlyCosts_ProjectMonth = $ProjectMonth_Last
    7. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
      8. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ProjectMonth over association MonthlyCosts_ProjectMonth from MonthlyCosts
      9. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable FirstOfTheMonth=parseDateTimeUTC('01'+'-'+$ProjectMonth/MonthName, 'dd-MM-yyyy')
      10. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change MonthlyCosts (StartDate=$FirstOfTheMonth, EndDate=addMonths(addDays($FirstOfTheMonth, -1), 1), PercentageInProjectResource=1; refreshInClient=false)
      11. END
    12. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
      13. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable LastMonthStartDate=parseDateTimeUTC(formatDateTimeUTC($ProjectResource/EndDate,'yyyy-MM')+'-01','yyyy-MM-dd')
      14. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable ReverseMultiplier=1 div $MonthlyCosts/PercentageInProjectResource
      15. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change MonthlyCosts (PercentageInProjectResource=1, FTE=$MonthlyCosts/FTE * $ReverseMultiplier; refreshInClient=false)
      16. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable DaysInProject_2=round(daysBetween($ProjectResource/EndDate,$LastMonthStartDate))+1
      17. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable DaysInMonth_3=round(daysBetween($LastMonthStartDate,addMonthsUTC($LastMonthStartDate,1)))
      18. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change MonthlyCosts (PercentageInProjectResource=$DaysInProject_2 div $DaysInMonth_3, FTE=$MonthlyCosts/FTE * $MonthlyCosts/PercentageInProjectResource; refreshInClient=false)
      19. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change MonthlyCosts (StartDate=$LastMonthStartDate, EndDate=$ProjectResource/EndDate; refreshInClient=false)
      20. END
  21. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    22. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable StartMonthStartDate=parseDateTimeUTC(formatDateTimeUTC($ProjectResource/StartDate,'yyyy-MM')+'-01','yyyy-MM-dd')
    23. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable DaysInMonthBeforeStarted=round(daysBetween($StartMonthStartDate,$ProjectResource/StartDate))
    24. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable DaysInMonth_2=round(daysBetween($StartMonthStartDate,addMonthsUTC($StartMonthStartDate,1)))
    25. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change MonthlyCosts (PercentageInProjectResource=1 - ( $DaysInMonthBeforeStarted div $DaysInMonth_2 ), FTE=if $MonthlyCosts/FTE > $MonthlyCosts/PercentageInProjectResource then $MonthlyCosts/FTE * $MonthlyCosts/PercentageInProjectResource else $MonthlyCosts/FTE; refreshInClient=false)
    26. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change MonthlyCosts (StartDate=$ProjectResource/StartDate, EndDate=addDays($ProjectResource/StartDate, $DaysInMonth_2-1); refreshInClient=false)
    27. END
28. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  29. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable StartandLastMonthStartDate=parseDateTimeUTC(formatDateTimeUTC($ProjectResource/StartDate,'yyyy-MM')+'-01','yyyy-MM-dd')
  30. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable DaysInProject=round(daysBetween($ProjectResource/StartDate,$ProjectResource/EndDate))+1
  31. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable DaysInMonth_1=round(daysBetween($StartandLastMonthStartDate,addMonthsUTC($StartandLastMonthStartDate,1)))
  32. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change MonthlyCosts (PercentageInProjectResource=$DaysInProject div $DaysInMonth_1, FTE=if $MonthlyCosts/FTE > $MonthlyCosts/PercentageInProjectResource then $MonthlyCosts/FTE * $MonthlyCosts/PercentageInProjectResource else $MonthlyCosts/FTE; refreshInClient=false)
  33. ACTION ChangeObjectAction: change MonthlyCosts (StartDate=$ProjectResource/StartDate, EndDate=$ProjectResource/EndDate; refreshInClient=false)
  34. END

    28. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=SumExternalCosts_Other, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
    29. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable SumExternalCostsBruto=$SumExternalCosts_Other
    30. REF ExclusiveMerge
31. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  32. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ExternalOverheadLine over association ProjectResource_ExternalOverheadLine from ProjectResource_Overhead
  33. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable SumExternalCostsBruto=($ExternalOverheadLine/OverheadPerFTEYear * $SumFTE div 12)
  34. END

FLOW Microflow: Projects.SUB_ProjectMonth_UpdateOverheadInternal
NODES=26; EDGES=20
1. START
2. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=SumInternalCostsBruto, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
3. DECISION Type of OverheadCalculation expression=$InternalCalculationRule/OverheadCalculation
4. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=DirectCosts
  5. DECISION Subcontracting? expression=$InternalCalculationRule/includeSubcontractingOverhead
  6. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
    7. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve MonthlyCostsList_EquipmentNoSC from Projects.MonthlyCosts
    8. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=SumExternalCosts_EquipmentNoSC, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
    9. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable SumInternalCostsBruto=$SumInternalCostsBruto + $SumExternalCosts_EquipmentNoSC
    10. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
    11. END
  12. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
    13. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve MonthlyCostsList_Equipment from Projects.MonthlyCosts
    14. ACTION AggregateListAction: AggregateListAction (output=SumExternalCosts_Equipment, errorHandlingType=Rollback)
    15. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable SumInternalCostsBruto=$SumInternalCostsBruto + $SumExternalCosts_Equipment
    16. REF ExclusiveMerge
17. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=(empty)
  18. REF ExclusiveMerge
19. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=FixedAmountFTEYear
  20. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve InternalOverheadLine over association ProjectResource_OverheadLine from ProjectResource_Overhead
  21. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable Indexation=if $InternalOverheadLine/IndexationPercentage != 0 and $InternalOverheadLine/IndexationPercentage != empty then (($InternalOverheadLine/IndexationPercentage div 100) + 1) else 1
  22. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable Year=parseInteger(getCaption($MonthlyCosts/Projects.MonthlyCosts_ProjectYear/Projects.ProjectYear/Year))
  23. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable IndexationYears=$Year - parseInteger(formatDateTime([%BeginOfCurrentDay%],'yyyy'))
  24. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable IndexationFactor=pow($Indexation,$IndexationYears)
  25. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable SumInternalCostsBruto=($InternalOverheadLine/OverheadPerFTEYear * $SumFTE div 12)*$IndexationFactor
  26. REF ExclusiveMerge

  25. ACTION ChangeListAction: change MonthlyCostsList_toCommit (type=Clear)

  27. ACTION JavaActionCallAction: call java action CommunityCommons.StartTransaction
  28. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Offset=$Offset + $Amount
  29. GOTO ExclusiveMerge // cycle

  31. END

FLOW Microflow: Projects.SUB_Project_RecalculateRoles
NODES=18; EDGES=16
1. START
2. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable StartTime=[%CurrentDateTime%]
3. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable Offset=0
4. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable Amount=500
5. NODE ExclusiveMerge: ExclusiveMerge
6. ACTION RetrieveAction: retrieve ProjectList from Projects.Project
7. DECISION Found? expression=$ProjectList != empty
8. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=false
  9. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable MicroflowTime=minutesBetween($StartTime, [%CurrentDateTime%])
  10. ACTION LogMessageAction: LogMessageAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  11. END
12. BRANCH when EnumerationCase=true
  13. LOOP iterate ProjectList as IteratorProject
    14. LOOP BODY
      15. ACTION MicroflowCallAction: call microflow Projects.Queue_Project_RecalculateAndPost
  16. ACTION ChangeListAction: change ProjectList (type=Clear)
  17. ACTION JavaActionCallAction: call java action CommunityCommons.EndTransaction
  18. ACTION JavaActionCallAction: call java action CommunityCommons.StartTransaction
  19. ACTION ChangeVariableAction: change variable Offset=$Offset + $Amount
  20. ACTION LogMessageAction: LogMessageAction (errorHandlingType=Rollback)
  21. GOTO ExclusiveMerge // cycle

FLOW Microflow: Projects.SUB_Project_RetrieveOrCreateFinalMonth
NODES=15; EDGES=11
1. START
2. ACTION CreateVariableAction: create variable StartMonthEndDate=parseDateTimeUTC(formatDateTimeUTC($Project/EndDate,'yyyy-MM')+'-01','yyyy-MM-dd')
3. ACTION CreateObjectAction: create Projects.ProjectMonth as FinalProjectMonth (Month=$Project/LastMonth, Year=$Project/LastYear, MonthName=replaceAll(toString($Project/LastMonth) + '-' + toString($Project/LastYear),'_',''), ProjectMonth_Project=$Project, ProjectMonth_Project_Last=$Project, PercentageInProject=(daysBetween($Project/EndDate,$StartMonthEndDate)+1) div daysBetween($StartMonthEndDate,addMonthsUTC($StartMonthEndDate,1)))
